 shrikrishna ne jab pragjyotishpur (vartmaan guwahati or aasapaas kaa ilaaka) ke raja nirkasur kaa vadh kiya to phir dwarka vaapasi ke darmyaan unhone balram se mithila main mulaakaat kii or unhen waapas lautne ke liye manaaya
 It is said that many of Balaram's companions settled in that region

Could this be the reason there is some similarity between Maithili and Gujarati, the languages of that region? Could some similarities in Maithili, Bangla, Nepali and Gujarati be rooted in that mythological event? It is a subject of intense research
 haalanki maujuuda itihaas lekhan lok-kathaon or lokgeeton ko bataur sakshya nakaarta he, lekin vidwaanon ko is disha main bhi kaam karnaa chahie
 Sama Chakeba and Samb's association with Mithila is around sama-chakeba's folk festival celebrated in Mithila, which is a symbol of unwavering love of brothers and sisters
 saamaa (yaa shyama!) krishna kii beti thi or samb kii bahan
 Sama was accused by Minister Churak (called Chugla) of having an illicit relationship with a sage, on which Krishna cursed Sama to become a bird
 baad main samb ne tapasya kar krishna ko is baat ke liye manaaya ki ve saamaa ko shraap mukt kare
 Krishna said that Sama will appear in human form once a year for eight days and at the same time the festival of sama-chakeba is celebrated
 lokgeeton main mantri churak (chugala) kii ninda kii jaati he or uski moonch main aag laga di jaati he
 Significantly, sama-chakeba starts on the Chharna day of Chhath and ends on the full moon day
 saamaa-chakeba mithila main hi manaaya jaataa he or chhath vrath ke bare main kehete hai ki asaadhya or gambhir rog jaise kusht, viklaangata, daag, badanaami, aapadaa ityadi ko dur karne kii prarthana kii jaati he
 Earlier we have described that Samb had leprosy for which Shakaldipi Brahmins were called from Shaka Island and who later settled in Magadha or resettled! There is something here that shows a finer connection between Samb, Leprosy, Gujarat (dwarka), Shakaldipi Brahmin, series of Sun-temples, Chhath and sama-chakeba
 haalanki yah prashn ab bhi anutarit he ki saamaa-chakeba kaa tyohaar sirf mithila main hi kyon manaaya jaataa he, gujarat yaa braj ke ilaakon main kyon nahin! kya braj yaa gujarat ke lokgeeton yaa desh ke anya ilaake main is tarah ke kisi parv ke sanket hai? sambhavat: ye sanket abhi tak nahin mili hai
 But the biggest thing is that if the Shakaldipi Brahmins had a role in it or under their influence the later kings built the Suryamandiras, then a question is still unanswered: the lack of mantras-rituals and priests in Chhath Puja and reverence by every section of the society
 To be celebrated with haalanki ek dharna buddha dharm se bhi sambandhit he
 Surya is also found in Buddhist and Hindu traditions and many Sun temples seem to have been built by kings who were also Buddhists
 to kya suryopasna kii koi aisi vidhi viksit kar di gai jo purohit or karmkand-viheen thi or jisane baad main chhath kaa rup le liya? ek katha ke mutabik, bahut sambhav he ki chhath puja ang-raaj kii karn kii vajah se lok-parv main parivartit ho gaya ho
 Karna had to bear the brunt of his life's thread and he prayed to the Sun to recognize himself
 karn kaa charitra ek vidroh kaa charitra he or aisa sambhav he ki parvarti pidiyon ne us vidroh ko ek pratik ke rup main purohit-viheen or karmkand viheen kar liya ho
 In Chhath Puja, the same things, fruits or products are used which are local
 lekin us drushti se dekhne par to lagata he ki chhath puja kii shuruyaat tab kii he jab maanav sabhyataa sirf fal-phool or kandamul par ji rahi tha or mithai bananaa nahin siikhaa tha yaa suvyavasthit kheti kaa vikaas nahin hua tha
 Varna system was not established in the society or was in its initial form
 kul milakar itnaa kaha ja saktaa he ki chhath parv samaajik samarasata or udaartaa kaa bada pratik parv he or shaayad yaheen isaki lokapriyata kaa kaaran bhi he
